  I just made minor changes for self-understanding. I don't claim authority of any class.

Data type for a code segment. Can be a regular segment, block of code
segments, a par statement (cobegin/coend) as well as while loops and if
statements.
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="2932" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="Seg"></a><a id="2937" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#2937" class="Datatype">Seg</a> <a id="2941" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2943" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="2947" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="LTL._==n_"></a><a id="4601" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#4601" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_==n_</a>        <a id="4614" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4616" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4617" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#4617" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="4619" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4621" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#1074" class="Datatype">NVar</a><a id="4625" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4627" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4629" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4630" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#4630" class="Bound">n</a> <a id="4632" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4634" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Nat.html#97" class="Datatype">ℕ</a><a id="4635" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4637" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4639" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#4027" class="Datatype">LTL</a>     <a id="4647" class="Comment">-- Nat variable x has the value n</a>
  <a id="LTL._==b_"></a><a id="4683" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#4683" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_==b_</a>        <a id="4696" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4698" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4699" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#4699" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="4701" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4703" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#1174" class="Datatype">BVar</a><a id="4707" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4709" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4711" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4712" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#4712" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="4714" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4716" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#1174" class="Datatype">BVar</a><a id="4720" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4722" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4724" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#4027" class="Datatype">LTL</a>  <a id="4729" class="Comment">-- Bool variable x has the value of y</a>
  <a id="LTL.isTrue"></a><a id="4769" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#4769" class="InductiveConstructor">isTrue</a>       <a id="4782" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4784" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4785" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#4785" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="4787" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4789" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#1174" class="Datatype">BVar</a><a id="4793" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4795" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4797" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#4027" class="Datatype">LTL</a>               <a id="4815" class="Comment">-- Variable x has the value -- true</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

## The LTL-rule data type

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="6738" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="LTLRule"></a><a id="6743" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#6743" class="Datatype">LTLRule</a> <a id="6751" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6753" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="6757" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="LTLRule.∧-e₁"></a><a id="6765" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#6765" class="InductiveConstructor">∧-e₁</a>   <a id="6772" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6774" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#4027" class="Datatype">LTL</a> <a id="6778" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6780" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#6743" class="Datatype">LTLRule</a>        <a id="6795" class="Comment">-- and-elimination on first element</a>
  <a id="LTLRule.∧-e₂"></a><a id="6833" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#6833" class="InductiveConstructor">∧-e₂</a>   <a id="6840" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6842" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#4027" class="Datatype">LTL</a> <a id="6846" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6848" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#6743" class="Datatype">LTLRule</a>        <a id="6863" class="Comment">-- and-elimination on second element</a>

## Propositional logic representation

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="10414" class="Comment">-- Representation of propositional logic</a>
<a id="10455" class="Comment">-- data Props : Set where</a>
<a id="10481" class="Comment">--   T ⊥         : Props</a>
<a id="10506" class="Comment">--   _∧_ _∨_ _⇒_ : Props → Props → Props</a>
<a id="10547" class="Comment">--   p&#39;          : ℕ → Props</a>
<a id="10576" class="Comment">--   ~_          : Props → Props</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

## Translator

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="10649" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Translator"></a><a id="10656" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#10656" class="Module">Translator</a> <a id="10667" class="Keyword">where</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Translator for concurrent programs. Translates program representations into
transition relations (TransRel). The relations keep track of the LTL-formulas
related to the program statements of the programs.

### Actions

Data type for actions, reference to what happened when translating the program

### Hoare-style Triples

Represents transition relations, < pre > action < post >, where pre is the
precondition of the program statement, action the reference to the type of
program statement, and post the postcondition of the statement.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="12025" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="TransRel"></a><a id="12030" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#12030" class="Datatype">TransRel</a> <a id="12039" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12041" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="12045" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="TransRel.&lt;_&gt;_&lt;_&gt;"></a><a id="12053" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#12053" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">&lt;_&gt;_&lt;_&gt;</a> <a id="12061" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12063" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12064" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#12064" class="Bound">c₁</a> <a id="12067" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12069" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#4027" class="Datatype">LTL</a><a id="12072" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="12074" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12076" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#11001" class="Datatype">Action</a> <a id="12083" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12085" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12086" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#12086" class="Bound">c₂</a> <a id="12089" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12091" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#4027" class="Datatype">LTL</a><a id="12094" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="12096" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12098" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#12030" class="Datatype">TransRel</a>  <a id="12108" class="Comment">-- Hoare-style Triple</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


Translates a program statement into the corresponding `TransRel`.
  * `l`: Program label of the program statement.
  * `Stm`: The program statement.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="transStm"></a><a id="12306" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#12306" class="Function">transStm</a> <a id="12315" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12317" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#957" class="Datatype">Label</a> <a id="12323" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12325" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#2457" class="Datatype">Stm</a> <a id="12329" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12331" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#12030" class="Datatype">TransRel</a>

Flattens a list of lists into a single list.

Converts a list of segments and a label, representing a single block segment,
into a list of `TransRel`. The result contains the representation of the program
flow.

* `p`: Label of the parent segment.
* `List Seg`: List of all child segments.

Converts a list of segments into a single `LTL`. The list represents all child
segments initiated by a parent `par` segment. The result is an `LTL` used as a
precondition in order to allow the parent segment to be considered executed.

Helper function for translate that uses different translation approaches
depending on the type of segment to be translated.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="15238" class="Symbol">{-#</a> <a id="15242" class="Keyword">TERMINATING</a> <a id="15254" class="Symbol">#-}</a> <a id="15258" class="Comment">-- used to guarantee that there is no infinite looping</a>

  <a id="16727" class="Comment">-- Translate the if statement</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


Translate function that takes a program and returns a list of TransRel.
The list consists of two parts, first the statement specific translations,
the second the program flow relations between the segments.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="translate"></a><a id="16991" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#16991" class="Function">translate</a> <a id="17001" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17003" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#3795" class="Record">Prog</a> <a id="17008" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="17010" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.List.html#80" class="Datatype">List</a> <a id="17015" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#12030" class="Datatype">TransRel</a>

## Rules to construct proofs

Contains rules to use when construction proofs. Also has functions to check if
rules are used legally. Used in ProofChecker

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="17280" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Rules"></a><a id="17287" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#17287" class="Module">Rules</a> <a id="17293" class="Keyword">where</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Data type for program rules, indexed with rule and `LTL`. Specifically for
proof-steps regarding the programs

                                             <a id="18184" class="Comment">-- control progression</a>
